***пролить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролить.html>проли́ть</a> (9404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>лить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пролить.html>проли́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prolítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проливать.html>пролива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spill</li>
<li>to shed <i>(light, tears, blood)</i></li></ol>

***проложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a> (8384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прокладывать.html>прокла́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(a road, pipe etc.)</i> to build, to construct, to lay
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> tunnɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive a tunnel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to clear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> чему́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> dorógu čemú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pave the way for smth</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> sebé dorógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to work/carve one's way; elbow one's way</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> putʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make a path/road; break a trail</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>пути́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> nóvyje putí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blaze new trails; pioneer</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to map
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:курс.html>курс</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a>, самолёта)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> kurs (súdna, samoljóta)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay a course</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to interlay <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>листа́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> knígu bélymi listámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to interleave a book</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проложить.html>проложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:копирка.html>копи́рку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>листа́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proložítʹ</b> kopírku méždu listámi bumági</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to insert carbon paper between the sheets of paper</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***проломить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проломить.html>проломи́ть</a> (13012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проломить.html>проломи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prolomítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прола́мывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break through, to penetrate, to pierce, to make a hole in</li>
<li>to fracture (one's skull)</li></ol>

***промазать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промазать.html>прома́зать</a> (19720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промазать.html>прома́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promázatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прома́зывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smear, to plaster, to anoint, to grease, to oil <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">properly, thoroughly; deep into</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to miss (the target)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прома́зывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">promázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mázatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***промах.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́мах</a> (10374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́мах</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prómax</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́маха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́махи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́махов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(when shooting or throwing)</i> miss</li>
<li>blunder, slip
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́мах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">datʹ prómax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">make a blunder</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:малый.html>ма́лый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>про́мах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on mályj ne prómax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he's nobody's fool; he knows what's what</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промашка.html>прома́шка</a> (22627)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промах.html>прома́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promáx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***промежуток.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промежуток.html>промежу́ток</a> (7543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">межу́ток</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mežútok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промежуток.html>промежу́ток</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promežútok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промежуток.html>промежу́тка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промежуток.html>промежу́тки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промежуток.html>промежу́тков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gap, interval, period, space, stretch, span (a distance in space)</li></ol>

***промелькнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнувший.html>промелькну́вший</a> (8345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнувший.html>промелькну́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promelʹknúvšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promelʹknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***промелькнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ть</a> (8345)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мелькнуть.html>мелькну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">melʹknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promelʹknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to flash, to fly by, to flit by
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promelʹknúli</b> dve nedéli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two weeks flew by</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promelʹknútʹ</b> v golové (o mýsli)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flash/flit through one's mind</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be perceptible
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ирония.html>иро́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jevó slováx <b>promelʹknúla</b> irónija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was a touch of irony in his words</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выражение.html>выраже́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промелькнуть.html>промелькну́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v vyražénii jevó licá <b>promelʹknúla</b> ulýbka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a smile flitted across his face</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:променять.html>променя́ть</a> (14556)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менять.html>меня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">menjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:променять.html>променя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проме́нивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exchange <i>(for)</i>, to trade <i>(for)</i>, to barter <i>(for)</i>, to truck <i>(for)</i></li>
<li>to change <i>(for)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:променять.html>променя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кукушка.html>куку́шку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ястреб.html>ястреба</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">promenjátʹ kukúšku na jastreba</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to give a lark to catch a kite, change bad for worse</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">-мени́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">-menítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***промозглый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промозглый.html>промо́зглый</a> (17288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́зглый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mózglyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rotten; damp <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of weather</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мзга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mzga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rot, mold, damp weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mъzga</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μύδος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múdos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dampness, rot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">mosach</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unclean</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">mussig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dirty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">mudas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rotten algae</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промозглый.html>промо́зглый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promózglyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)промо́зглее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)промо́зглей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>piercingly cold and damp</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Short forms are sometimes avoided due to their similarity to past-tense forms of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">промо́згнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promózgnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to get wet and spoil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (especially the feminine and neuter singular <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промозглый.html>промо́згла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:промозглый.html>промо́згло</a></span>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***промокать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промокать.html>промока́ть</a> (28944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promóknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокать.html>промока́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promokátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get wet/soaked, to be soaking, to be sopping wet</li>
<li>to let water <i>(through)</i>, to not be impervious to water, to not be waterproof
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промокать.html>промока́ет</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождя́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto palʹtó <b>promokájet</b> (ot doždjá)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">this coat lets rainwater through, this coat is not rainproof</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрый.html>мо́крый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mókryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрота.html>мокрота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mokrotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мокрова́тый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mokrovátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочить.html>мочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">močítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:намочить.html>намочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">namočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промокну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">promoknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***промокнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кнуть</a> (8378)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокнуть.html>мо́кнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">móknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">promóknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:промокать.html>промока́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to get wet/soaked, to be soaking, to be sopping wet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кнуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>косте́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>promóknutʹ</b> do kostéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get soaked to the bone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:промокнуть.html>промо́кло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насквозь.html>наскво́зь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">palʹtó <b>promóklo</b> naskvózʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to the coat is soaking wet; the coat is wet through</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to let water <i>(through)</i>, to not be impervious to water, to not be waterproof</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрый.html>мо́крый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mókryj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрота.html>мокрота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mokrotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мокрова́тый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mokrovátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочить.html>мочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">močítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:намочить.html>намочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">namočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamočítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочка.html>мо́чка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">móčka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
